[@商店套]
{

#IF
#ACT
MOV N888 <$STR(N0)>

#if
Equal <$ItemInfo[$STR(N888)].Color> 158
#act
GOTO @商店套1
break
#ELSEACT

#if
Equal <$ItemInfo[$STR(N888)].Color> 155
#act
GOTO @妖玛套
break
#ELSEACT

#if
Equal <$ItemInfo[$STR(N888)].Color> 168
#act
GOTO @祖玛套
break
#ELSEACT

#if
Equal <$ItemInfo[$STR(N888)].Color> 116
#act
GOTO @赤月套
break
#ELSEACT

#if
Equal <$ItemInfo[$STR(N888)].Color> 132
#act
GOTO @魔龙套
break
#ELSEACT

#if
Equal <$ItemInfo[$STR(N888)].Color> 19
#act
GOTO @飞仙套
break
#ELSEACT

#if
Equal <$ItemInfo[$STR(N888)].Color> 24
#act
GOTO @强仙套
break
#ELSEACT

#if
Equal <$ItemInfo[$STR(N888)].Color> 244
#act
GOTO @成仙套
break
#ELSEACT

#if
Equal <$ItemInfo[$STR(N888)].Color> 58
#act
GOTO @灭世套
break
#ELSEACT


#if
CHECKTEXTLIST <$str(S0)> ../QuestDiary/游戏配置/灵宠配置/灵宠列表.txt
#act
MOV S888 <$str(S0)>
MOV N888 <$STR(N0)>
MOV N799 <$ItemInfo[$STR(N888)].Color>



#IF
CHECKTEXTLIST <$str(S0)> ../QuestDiary/游戏配置/灵宠配置/灵宠列表.txt
NOT EQUAL N799 253
#ACT
MOV N889 [$灵宠身份铭牌基数]
INC N889 <$STR(G889)>
INC G889 1
HookItemIdx <$STR(N888)>
ChangeGiveItem 18 2 =<$STR(N889)>
ChangeGiveItem 8
ADDTEXTLIST 玩家：<$USERNAME>，灵宠名字：<$STR(S888)>，编号：<$STR(N889)> ../QuestDiary/游戏配置/灵宠配置/灵宠归属档案/<$STR(N889)>.txt
goto @宠物拾取鉴定
break
#ELSEACT

[@宠物拾取鉴定]
#IF
CHECKTEXTLIST <$str(S888)> ../QuestDiary/游戏配置/灵宠配置/灵宠成长值一档.txt
#ACT
GOTO @成长值一档
BREAK

#IF
CHECKTEXTLIST <$str(S888)> ../QuestDiary/游戏配置/灵宠配置/灵宠成长值二档.txt
#ACT
GOTO @成长值二档
BREAK

#IF
CHECKTEXTLIST <$str(S888)> ../QuestDiary/游戏配置/灵宠配置/灵宠成长值三档.txt
#ACT
GOTO @成长值三档
BREAK

#IF
CHECKTEXTLIST <$str(S888)> ../QuestDiary/游戏配置/灵宠配置/灵宠成长值四档.txt
#ACT
GOTO @成长值四档
BREAK

#IF
CHECKTEXTLIST <$str(S888)> ../QuestDiary/游戏配置/灵宠配置/灵宠成长值五档.txt
#ACT
GOTO @成长值五档
BREAK


#IF
CHECKTEXTLIST <$str(S888)> ../QuestDiary/游戏配置/灵宠配置/灵宠成长值六档.txt
#ACT
GOTO @成长值六档
BREAK

#IF
CHECKTEXTLIST <$str(S888)> ../QuestDiary/游戏配置/灵宠配置/灵宠成长值七档.txt
#ACT
GOTO @成长值七档
BREAK



[@成长值七档]
;//死神档次
#ACT
MOVR N800 [$七档灵宠最低资质] [$七档灵宠最高资质]
MOVR N801 [$七档灵宠最低资质] [$七档灵宠最高资质]
MOVR N802 [$七档灵宠最低资质] [$七档灵宠最高资质]

ADDTEXTLIST <$STR(N800)> ../QuestDiary/游戏配置/灵宠配置/灵宠攻击资质/<$STR(N889)>.txt

INC N800 <$STR(N802)>
